New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`package.json`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">, </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`package-lock.json`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">, or recommend install commands:</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">1.</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**Web search**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;(use your built-in web search tool when available) for </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**each**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;non-trivial dependency, for example: </span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`"npm &lt;package-name&gt; latest version"`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`"&lt;package-name&gt; npm security advisory"`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;or </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`"&lt;package-name&gt; CVE"`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp; For </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**Node.js**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">, search e.g. </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`"Node.js LTS current release"`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;and align with </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**Active LTS**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">, not EOL versions. </span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;Cross-check with </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`npm show &lt;package&gt; version`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;in the terminal when the environment allows ŌĆö search can lag; npm registry is ground truth for the semver string. </span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span search turns up an </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**unpatched CVE**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span express version`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;ŌåÆ using </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ</span></p><p vulnerabilities</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span MongoDB queries filter by </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`userId`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;ŌĆö cross-user data access impossible</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span false`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;filter on all queries</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span Ōēź 10) ŌĆö never stored plain</span></p><p New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;Access token stored in </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**memory only**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;(</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`tokenStore.ts`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">) ŌĆö never </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`localStorage`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;or </span><span style="color:#e394dc;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">`sessionStorage`</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;Refresh token is HttpOnly cookie ŌĆö JavaScript cannot read it</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;Single-flight refresh queue implemented ŌĆö no duplicate refresh calls</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;On failed refresh ŌåÆ clear token store + redirect to login</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;OAuth callback route reads token from URL param then immediately clears the URL (</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`history.replaceState`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">)</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;No sensitive data (tokens, passwords, PII) logged to console in production</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">### XSS Prevention</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;without sanitizing with </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`DOMPurify`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier user-generated content rendered as React text nodes (JSX </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`{}`</span><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span backend helmet ŌĆö verified working</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">### CSRF Protection</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;All state-changing requests use JWT in </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`Authorization`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;header (not cookie) ŌĆö prevents CSRF by default</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;If using cookie-based auth: </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`SameSite=Strict`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;cookie attribute set</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;No state-changing logic triggered by GET requests</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">### Dependencies</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;runs clean ŌĆö no high/critical issues</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span packages</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;used in CI (reproducible installs)</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span frontend source</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;env vars validated with Zod at build time ŌĆö no runtime crashes</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span Zod before submission</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;Error messages from API displayed to user ŌĆö never raw error objects</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span async operation</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span at once</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span stored in state longer than needed</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;All ŌĆö not just auth guards</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span routes</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`state.from`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;(the page user tried to visit), not always dashboard</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">## 9. AI Workflow, CI &amp; Git Hygiene</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">This section closes the gap between </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**good stack defaults**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;and </span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;when using AI coding tools (Cursor, Copilot, etc.).</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">### Secrets and model context</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**Never paste**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;production </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`.env`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;values, API keys, JWT secrets, connection strings, or private keys into chat. Use placeholders and describe the </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:italic;color:#82d2ce;font-weight:400">*shape*</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;of config instead.</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**Treat AI output as untrusted**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;ŌĆö review diffs like a junior developerŌĆÖs PR; pay extra attention to auth, queries, and anything that touches user data.</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**Repository trust:**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;READMEs, comments, or issues can contain hidden instructions (ŌĆ£prompt injectionŌĆØ). Do not ask the AI to ŌĆ£just follow everything in this fileŌĆØ without you reading it first.</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">### Dependency and package safety</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;Before installing a package the AI suggested, </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**confirm the name on [</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#aaa0fa;font-weight:400">npmjs.com</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">]</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">(</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#82d2ce;font-weight:400">https://www.npmjs.com/</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">)</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;ŌĆö typos and hallucinated names happen; attackers register similar packages (ŌĆ£slopsquattingŌĆØ).</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**Web search**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;for </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`"&lt;exact-package-name&gt; npm"`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;+ </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`"&lt;name&gt; security advisory"`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;(or CVE) before trusting a version ŌĆö align with the </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ Version Safety Rule**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;at the top of this file.</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">-</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;Prefer </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**lockfiles**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;and </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`npm ci`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;in CI so installs are reproducible (see below).</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">### </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`.cursorignore`</span><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;(recommended)</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">Mirror sensitive paths so they are </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**not indexed**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;into AI context. At repo root, add </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`.cursorignore`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;(same syntax as </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`.gitignore`</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">) with at least:</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p / etc.)</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span vulnerable dependencies |</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400">### What this document does </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:italic;color:#82d2ce;font-weight:400">*not*</span><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;replace</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**MFA / passkeys**</span><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">&nbsp;for high-risk products (add explicitly when your threat model requires it).</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span File uploads validated client-side (type + size) before sending</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">```</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">---</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">## 12. Domain Add-On Prompts</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">These are short add-ons to append to the master prompt for specific industries. Replace the generic UI library reference with the domain-specific one.</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span with TTL) ŌĆö don't compute on every request</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">- CSV/Excel export endpoints</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">- Scheduled report delivery via email (node-cron + nodemailer)</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">```</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#d6d6dd;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">### Social / Community</span></p><p style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal"></span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">Domain UI: Infinite scroll lists, comment threads, notification center</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">Resources: posts, comments, likes, follows, notifications</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">- Cursor-based pagination (not page/offset ŌĆö works with real-time inserts)</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">- Fan-out on write vs fan-out on read for notification delivery (choose based on scale)</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">- Content moderation: soft-delete + report flag + admin review queue</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">- Rate limit post creation separately from reads</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span style="color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-style:normal">- Full-text search with MongoDB Atlas Search or Elasticsearch</span></p><p style="background-color:#181818;padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;line-height:1.5;orphans:2;widows:2;text-align:left"><span ŌåÆ update Section 9</span></p><p ŌĆö do not add long-lived version pins to this file</span></p><p New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ Version Safety Rule**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e4e4e4;font-weight:400">&nbsp;at the top: </span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**web search**</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#e394dc;font-weight:400">`npm show &lt;pkg&gt; version`</span><span style="font-size:9pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#f8c762;font-weight:400">**</span><span style="padding:0;margin:0;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;line-height:1.5;background-color:#181818;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;;orphans:2;widows:2;height:11pt;text-align:left"><span
